            @CountryID uniqueidentifier,
            @Address nvarchar(200),
            @ReceiveNewsLetters bit
            )
            AS BEGIN
	        UPDATE [dbo].[Persons]
            SET
		        PersonID = @PersonID,
		        PersonName = @PersonName,
		        Email = @Email,
		        DateOfBirth = @DateOfBirth,
		        Gender = @Gender,
		        CountryID = @CountryID,
		        Address = @Address,
		        ReceiveNewsLetters = @ReceiveNewsLetters
	        WHERE PersonID = @PersonID
            END
